# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 01:05:36.505005

### Base Program

```py
def maximum_children_with_eight_dollars(money, children):
    if money < children * 1 or money > children * 8:
        return -1
    max_eights = (money - children) // 7
    return children if max_eights >= children else max_eights
```

### Input

```json
[44, 35]
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def maximum_children_with_eight_dollars(money, children):
    if money < children * 1 or money > children * 8:
        return -1
    max_eights = (money - children) // 7
    return children if max_eights >= children else max_eights
```

<details>
<summary>parser endpoint: passed ✅</summary>

Message: 
```
Success
```

Actual Output: 
```json
{
    "importStatements": [],
    "fncs": {
        "maximum_children_with_eight_dollars": {
            "name": "maximum_children_with_eight_dollars",
            "rettype": "*",
            "initloc": 1,
            "endloc": 0,
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def maximum_children_with_eight_dollars(var_0, var_1):
    if var_0 < var_1 * 1 or var_0 > var_1 * 8:
        return -1
    max_eights = (var_0 - var_1) // 7
    return var_1 if max_eights >= var_1 else max_eights
```

<summary>parser endpoint: passed ✅</summary>

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def maximum_children_with_eight_dollars(money, children):
    if money < children or money > 8 * children:
        return -1
    max_eights = (money + -children) // 7
    return children if max_eights >= children else max_eights
```

<details>
<summary>parser endpoint: passed ✅</summary>

Message: 
```
Success
```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py
def maximum_children_with_eight_dollars(var_2, var_3):
    if var_2 < var_3 or var_2 > 8 * var_3:
        return -1
    max_eights = (var_2 + -var_3) // 7
    return var_3 if max_eights >= var_3 else max_eights
```
